# Resume Tailoring Assistance

**USER**:
I need help fine-tuning my resume by condensing the verbiage and tailoring the bullets to a specific job. How would you like me to present the information to you?

---

**ASSISTANT**:
Of course, I&#x27;d be happy to help you fine-tune your resume! To get started, please provide me with the following information:

1. Your current resume or a list of your work experiences, including job titles, companies, and dates.
2. The specific job description or job title you&#x27;re tailoring your resume for.
3. Any key skills or qualifications mentioned in the job description.
4. Any specific accomplishments or projects you&#x27;d like to highlight.
5. Any other relevant information you think should be included.

Feel free to provide the information in any format that&#x27;s convenient for you, such as bullet points or paragraphs. Once I have the details, we can work together to condense the verbiage and tailor the content to match the job you&#x27;re targeting.

2. Manager, Professional Services
Job Description
WHAT IS BOX?
Box is the market leader for Cloud Content Management. Our mission is to power how the world works together. Box is partnering with enterprise organizations to accelerate their digital transformation by creating a single platform for secure content management, collaboration and workflow. We have an amazing opportunity to further establish ourselves as leaders in the space, and we need strong advocates to help us achieve that goal. By joining Box, you will have the unique opportunity to help capture a majority of this developing market and define what content management looks like for the digital enterprise. Today, Box powers 100,000+ businesses, including many top Fortune 500 companies who trust our secure collaboration platform to manage the entire content lifecycle.
 
WHY BOX NEEDS YOU
Box Consulting is a fast growing team helping customers rapidly deploy, maximize value, and deeply integrate Box into their enterprises. Your proven ability to work creatively and analytically on complex, multi phase engagements with the most strategic of customers will help you build, manage, and scale your team in highly engaged environment.  Excellent communication, leadership, and management skills enable you to grow the team&#x27;s professional development while staying highly engaged with customers - an opportunity for your team to learn the depth of your delivery expertise on the job.

Box is growing fast. Real fast. Every business in the world is looking to modernize the way they work. As the leader in cloud content management, Box is the only company that can help enterprises transform how people work together.  Your years of experience with project management and business process design, combined with expert knowledge of internal processes and related systems, empower you to be an influential leader within Box Consulting and more broadly across all of Box.

WHAT YOU&#x27;LL DO

As a Manager, you will be scaling a world-class team, working closely with our customers as a thought leader, shape &amp; evolve consulting delivery offerings, and drive new business with your sales partners.  You will bring the energy and expertise to inspire our customers and influence Box Consulting&#x27;s strategic direction.  You will lead teams of varying levels of experience, thrive in dynamic &amp; cross-functional environments, and enjoy achieving results thru engaging directly with our customers.

WHO YOU ARE

You have solid people management experience, including recruiting, hiring, onboarding as well as cultivating professional development opportunities as part of performance management functions
6+ years service delivery experience; preferably projects with significant impact to the financial performance of the organization
Knowledge of sales operations processes, technologies and organizations; solid understanding of revenue performance targets, utilization objectives, industry standard key performance indicators
Regularly interacts with and influences senior management, other functional areas such as Sales and/or external parties
Works autonomously with limited guidance - Strong sense of urgency for customer issues. Comfortable leading larger teams including cross-functional members
Implements robust strategies to effectively manage the team; uncovers improvement areas and develops clear, actionable development plans to achieve full range of goals 
Focuses on maximizing customer delight and outcomes in all conversations across Box; consistent advocacy of customer experience cross functionally with all levels of leadership
Proven track record or experience working effectively with sales leaders to help identify opportunities, present solutions during a sales cycle, and contribute to the sales estimation and contracting
Head-over-heels about this role — but not sure you meet all the requirements? Apply anyway! Studies have shown that women and people of color are less likely to apply to jobs unless they meet every single qualification. At Box, we take a big-picture approach to hiring that fosters authenticity, diversity, and inclusion. If you&#x27;re passionate about this opportunity, chances are, you shine pretty bright.

**USER**:
Keep in mind also that before this work history, I was in the army for 14 years. This was briefly mentioned in the original resume summary. The last 6 years up to 2013 were spent in the 7th special forces group as a 255AP Chief Information Systems Technician warrant officer leading major projects. I will paste a full history of that work for you to condense and make it work for this job description

CHIEF INFORMATION SYSTEMS TECHNICIAN (255AP) JUL 2008 - NOV 2013
U.S. Army, 7th Special Forces Group Eglin Air Force Base, FL
● Led Special Ops IT Teams, Executive Technical Advisor; Maintained &amp; fortified information systems of the
highest classifications. Trained co-workers and provided direct support for sensitive TS/SCI missions
○ Migrated Combined &amp; Joint Special Forces CLASSIFIED SharePoint Services 3.0 to SharePoint Server 2007 to a new
server farm with less than 1% data loss
○ Managed over 800 local and remote user accounts while leading a migration team moving equipment and
Active Directory services to a new server farm; upgraded Windows Server 2003 to virtual Windows Server
2008 resulting in early and seamless transfer of all enterprise digital services
○ Mitigated risk by migrating over 2 Terabytes of data on direct-attached storage devices to a Distributed File
System of servers and network-attached storage devices
○ Transferred operational e-mail services to a new server farm and upgraded MS Exchange 2003 to Exchange
2007 with associated MS SQL servers with no data loss and minimal downtime for over 800 e-mail accounts
○ Led a team of 19 Soldiers, Sailors, and Airmen as the Deputy Information Management Officer (IMO) for the
Combined Joint Special Operations Task Force – Afghanistan (CJSOTF-A) with over 800 Army, Air Force,
Marine, and Coalition partners
○ Managed and Provided CLASSIFIED, UNCLASSIFIED, Coalition, and Voice Over IP (VoIP) Networks to 48 remote
sites in Afghanistan by hub-spoke Very Small Aperture Terminal (VSAT) network using HAIPE type 1 encryption
○ Performed forensics analysis of confiscated computers using open-source data recovery techniques

cover letter:
Dear Eightfold Hiring Team,

I am excited to express my interest in the Customer Success Manager position at Eightfold. My journey, combining a dedicated pursuit of knowledge in technology, ecological and human resilience, with a diverse background as a soldier, technician, consultant, and sales professional, aligns seamlessly with Eightfold’s mission to help everyone see their full potential and find the right job.

Intrigued by Eightfold’s commitment to providing actionable insights for jobseekers, I am driven by a profound desire to contribute to both planetary and humanitarian well-being through the integration of people and their essential information. Rooted in an unwavering commitment to leave a positive impact, I possess a unique ability to bridge functional aspects with design principles and human understanding.

My most recent role included intensive training as a Solution Consultant, refining my skills in storytelling, value-driven selling, customer success, and presentation — competencies cultivated during previous sales positions and entrepreneurial ventures.

Key strengths I bring to the table:

14 years in the military, with 6 years in Special Operations
A decade of IT project management, including complex organizational transitions
4 years of consultative sales experience spanning diverse industries
Advanced education in records management and office systems technology
Proficiency in communication, editing, presentation, and reporting
Sound planning and operations acumen honed through education and hands-on experience

In my previous role, I received recognition for fostering inclusivity and leading with empathy, showcasing my ability to establish strong relationships with clients while consistently delivering exceptional value. The most exciting aspect of my last company when I started there was their acquisition of an end-to-end talent operation platform. I saw this as my opportunity to help people find out what they’re made of and where they belonged. The integration of this platform was perpetually delayed. I see a far more advanced and capable opportunity in the Eightfold platform. I am eager to take command and help the masses achieve success in their purpose-defining job seeking journey.

Having led in the military and Team Rubicon, I am adept at building and nurturing cohesive teams focused on achieving objectives. As a Clay Hunt Fellow at Team Rubicon, I underwent immersive leadership development that honed my ability to navigate challenges and lead with confidence. Through specialized training and hands-on disaster relief, I cultivated adaptability, critical decision-making, and effective communication, equipping me to guide diverse teams in high-pressure situations.

I am eager to contribute my expertise to the Eightfold team, known for its commitment to excellence. My track record of effective communication and maintaining high standards align well with the role of a Customer Success Manager. I would be honored to contribute my skills and insights to your team.

Please feel free to contact me at (737) 234-0110 or george@xmize.com to discuss this opportunity in further detail.

Sincerely,

George Steward


job description:
Eightfold was founded with a vision to solve for employment in our society. For decades, the connection between individuals and opportunities has been based on who the individuals are and the strength of their network, vs. their potential. Eightfold leverages artificial intelligence to transform how to think about skills and capabilities for individuals as well as how jobs and career decisions are made. Eightfold offers the industry’s first AI-powered Talent Intelligence Platform to transform how organizations plan, hire, develop and retain a diverse workforce, enabling individuals to transform their career. 
 
To date, Eightfold AI has received more than $410 million in funding and a valuation of over $2B from leading investors to further our mission of finding the right career for everyone in the world. If you are passionate about solving one of the most fundamental challenges of our society - employment, working on hard business problems and being part of an amazing growth story - Eightfold is the place to be!
 
About the Role
The Customer Success Manager role at Eightfold is responsible for our customers&#x27; post-sales and implementation journey, focusing on helping them achieve their business outcomes and continually driving value from the Eightfold Talent Intelligence Platform. Our Customer Success Managers share best practices and play-books to help our customers scale adoption and usage while achieving their goals. 
 
The Customer Success Manager will become a trusted advisor to help our customers navigate the digital transformation landscape. You will help them define their key aspirations and leverage the power of big data, AI and deep machine learning to re-design the way they acquire, engage and empower talent, internally and externally, across the globe. You will also be the voice of our customers back to Eightfold. 
 
Your day to day (Responsibilities)
Evangelize Eightfold products with our customers and ensure customers maximize product value 
Monitor product adoption &amp; business outcomes; identify opportunities for improved usage &amp; impact, and see those opportunities through with your customer
Unblock internal escalations by partnering with cross functional teams including product, engineering, product delivery, support, and sales
Build a deep understanding of your customer’s business and HR challenges; serve as a thought partner on strategy development and the role Eightfold can play. 
Build relationships and credibility with key contacts at all levels; proactively identify contact gaps and work cross-functionally to foster those new relationships
Stay abreast of Eightfold product releases, roadmap, and the broader HR Tech landscape
Influence Eightfold’s strategic direction by understanding customer’s business, challenges, desired outcomes, and requested product features
Drive customer satisfaction through impeccable execution &amp; strategic value add, guaranteeing customer renewal
 
Must haves:
3+ years of experience in management consulting, functional HR talent acquisition/talent management/learning/etc., customer success, or account management
 
Nice to haves:
8+ years of experience in management consulting, functional HR talent acquisition/talent management/learning/etc., customer success, or account management
Experience in AI/ML technologies in the HR space or working at a fast-growing technology/SaaS company
Excellent problem solving in complex, multi-stakeholder situations
Top-level data analysis and synthesis
Close attention to detail, basics of project management, and ability to keep multiple trains running at once
Strong verbal and written communication skills
Experience with public speaking, webinars, and conferences

As my confidence grew, I naturally excelled in communicating with individuals from various locations and backgrounds. A decade of diverse experiences has cultivated my comfort and confidence in the communication skills vital for success in this social impact consultant role. 4 years of consultative sales experience across diverse industries

Sound planning and operations acumen honed through education and hands-on experience

Want to work for a mission driven company that digitally maps soil with machine learning to help sustainably produce food and reverse climate change?  EarthOptics is a growing AgTech company developing tools that help farmers more sustainably manage their soil, increase yields and feed the growing world.  We are seeking a Field Operations Business Manager to join our team.  As a Field Operations Business Manager you will have people management and individual contributor responsibilities as you lead and manage the business analytics function along with multiple departments including scheduling, inventory, and asset/maintenance management. Your primary responsibility will be to ensure the smooth operation of these areas, aligning them with the organization&#x27;s goals and objectives. This role requires strategic thinking, strong leadership abilities, and the capacity to foster collaboration across departments.



A Day in the Life…

A day in the life of a Field Operations Business Manager is a dynamic blend of strategic leadership and hands-on management. They begin by refining inventory control processes, optimizing stock levels, and ensuring efficient asset utilization. Assist with budget management and resource allocation as they navigate financial targets. Armed with data-driven insights, they continuously improve operations through refined KPIs and metrics, all while providing mentorship, fostering collaboration, and ensuring compliance across departments. Serving as a link between analytics and operations, they communicate performance through reports, all while upholding safety standards and EarthOptics&#x27; cultural values. Their day exemplifies a commitment to operational excellence and a thriving, values-driven workplace.



We seek motivated individuals who are eager to gain new skills in a fast-paced environment, and work closely and collaboratively with a team.  We are committed to building a diverse team of employees from various backgrounds, educational histories, and industries. We have a competitive compensation package including robust healthcare benefits, paid time off and meaningful equity options grants. Even if you do not meet all of the requirements below, we encourage you to apply - we’d love to hear from you!  Learn more at www.EarthOptics.com.



To learn more about working at EarthOptics, visit: https://www.themuse.com/profiles/earthoptics 



Job Type: Full-Time, Exempt

Work Location: Remote

Travel:  10%

Compensation: &quot;The anticipated base salary for this position is expected to be within this range: $60,200 to $110,000. Your actual base pay will depend on your geographic location–EarthOptics uses compensation regions that vary depending on location. Individual pay is also determined by job-related skills, experience, and relevant education or training. Your recruiter can share more about the specific salary range for your preferred location during the hiring process.&quot;



Supervisory Responsibilities:

Develop and implement inventory control processes, including forecasting, procurement, storage, and distribution, to optimize stock levels, minimize costs, and prevent out-of-stock or excess inventory.
Create strategies for effective management and utilization of company assets, tracking and maintaining schedules to ensure optimal performance and extend asset lifespan.
Prepare and manage budgets for inventory, asset, procurement, and maintenance departments, ensuring optimal allocation of resources and adherence to financial targets.
Develop key performance indicators (KPIs) and performance metrics to assess the efficiency and effectiveness of inventory, asset, procurement, maintenance, and scheduling functions, regularly monitoring and analyzing data to identify areas for improvement.
Provide guidance, support, and mentorship to departmental teams, ensuring effective communication, collaboration, and coordination across departments.


Duties &amp; Responsibilities:

Serve as a point of contact for business analytics-related inquiries, providing guidance and support to internal stakeholders and fostering strong working relationships.
Prepare regular reports, presentations, and updates on inventory, asset, procurement, maintenance, and scheduling performance for senior management, stakeholders, and other relevant parties.
Ensure compliance with safety guidelines, company policies, and regulatory requirements, promoting a safe work environment.
Practice and encourage the cultural concepts and values of EarthOptics: autonomy and accountability, recognition and respect, information and intent.


What we are looking for:

Bachelor&#x27;s degree in Business Administration, Operations Management, or a related field
Previous supervisory experience and proven ability to motivate and manage distributed teams
Proven experience in operations management with a strong knowledge of inventory management, asset tracking, procurement, and maintenance best practices.
Strong leadership skills with the ability to inspire and motivate teams.
Excellent analytical and problem-solving abilities.
Solid understanding of financial management and budgeting principles.
Excellent written and verbal communication skills
Exceptional interpersonal and customer service skills
Strong analytical skills and problem-solving skills
Ability to prioritize tasks and to delegate them when appropriate
Ability to learn and use new technologies
Proficient with Google Suite and Slack


We are interested in every qualified candidate who is eligible to work in the continental United States. However, we are not able to sponsor or transfer visas at this time.



What would make you stand out:

Previous roles such as Inventory Manager, Asset Manager, Operations Manager, Procurement Manager, or Supply Chain Manager
Experience in budgeting, financial management, and resource allocation
Candidates with a track record of implementing effective KPIs and performance metrics, as well as fostering cross-departmental collaboration

Thank you I like what you did. Please provide another version and use this company description for more context on the company and how I can help them achieve their goals and accomplish their mission

Clean Scapes Landscaping provides full-service commercial landscaping, specializing in the construction and maintenance of softscape, hardscape, and irrigation. Founded in 2005 by a core group of landscape professionals, we are one of Texas&#x27;​ finest landscaping leaders.

With our decades-long experience, we bring out the full beauty and creativity of a landscape’s design while providing attention to each detail. We are trusted to accommodate landscape projects of any size and can provide a multi-million dollar bonding capacity. More importantly, we are committed to the safety and well-being of all by adhering to a comprehensive safety program, reinforced by regular meetings, full training for new employees, and requirements that each crew member be outfitted with needed safety equipment.

As we endeavor to be the best guardian of each landscape, we know the importance of being vigilant environmental stewards. With this in mind, we source materials locally and use native plants to reduce irrigation needs. These practices are incorporated into our many LEED registered projects. Additionally, we are Green Garden Certified with the City of Austin to promote sustainable and environmentally-sound landscape practices. Furthering our commitment to the environment, we are stakeholders in the Central Texas Clean Cities Coalition. As such, we have converted our large mowers from gasoline-powered to propane-powered to reduce emissions and improve local air quality.

Our many clients—representing retail, office, mixed-use, multifamily, healthcare, education, civic, and resort properties—are confident in our abilities, professionalism, and history of delivering results. By continuing to meet and exceed expectations, we are building upon existing relationships and cultivating new ones.

Clean Scapes Landscaping provides full-service commercial landscaping, specializing in the construction and maintenance of softscape, hardscape, and irrigation. Founded in 2005 by a core group of landscape professionals, we are one of Texas&#x27;​ finest landscaping leaders.

With our decades-long experience, we bring out the full beauty and creativity of a landscape’s design while providing attention to each detail. We are trusted to accommodate landscape projects of any size and can provide a multi-million dollar bonding capacity. More importantly, we are committed to the safety and well-being of all by adhering to a comprehensive safety program, reinforced by regular meetings, full training for new employees, and requirements that each crew member be outfitted with needed safety equipment.

As we endeavor to be the best guardian of each landscape, we know the importance of being vigilant environmental stewards. With this in mind, we source materials locally and use native plants to reduce irrigation needs. These practices are incorporated into our many LEED registered projects. Additionally, we are Green Garden Certified with the City of Austin to promote sustainable and environmentally-sound landscape practices. Furthering our commitment to the environment, we are stakeholders in the Central Texas Clean Cities Coalition. As such, we have converted our large mowers from gasoline-powered to propane-powered to reduce emissions and improve local air quality.

Our many clients—representing retail, office, mixed-use, multifamily, healthcare, education, civic, and resort properties—are confident in our abilities, professionalism, and history of delivering results. By continuing to meet and exceed expectations, we are building upon existing relationships and cultivating new ones.

Now, here is the actual job description to further hone in the content of the letter with the context of what I have to offer.

Funga is a seed stage public benefit corporation harnessing forest fungal networks to address the climate crisis. We combine modern DNA sequencing and machine learning technology with breakthrough research on the forest microbiome to put the right native, biodiverse communities of mycorrhizal fungi in the right place. This leads to more quality wood created more quickly, more carbon sequestered, and more resilient forests. We serve land partners seeking to implement regenerative forestry practices that improve productivity and sustainability, and corporate carbon buyers building high-quality carbon removal portfolios with strong social and biodiversity outcomes. We’re a team of passionate scientists and builders on a mission to draw down at least three gigatons of carbon dioxide from the atmosphere by 2050.

​

About the Role
Over the next six to 12 months we will be growing our team, scaling up our administrative functions, and installing a headquarters in Austin, TX. We are seeking an organized, relationship-oriented administrator passionate about climate solutions to provide in-person support to the team as we grow.

​

If you are excited by starting new things, learning as you go, and being hands-on in applying your experience to the climate crisis, you will dig working with us. We encourage you to apply even if only some of the below criteria are met - just make sure to tell us why you’re excited about Funga!

​

What You Will Do
Executive support: Build close relationships with Funga’s leadership team and provide timely support through email and scheduling management, digital organization, and relationship management with employees, partners, and customers.

Company administration: Support our vendor relationships including bookkeepers, payroll and benefits, legal counsel, insurance and utility providers. Financial administration: Support company financial management activities including payroll, budget management, expense reporting, invoice tracking and payment, quarterly and annual board financial reporting.

Recruiting: Support hiring managers with development of job descriptions, job posting, candidate review and interview scheduling, offer letters, employment verification, and onboarding.

Manage our office: Establish and support the functioning of a productive office environment including utility and cleaning schedule management, office maintenance, ordering of supplies, equipment and inventory management. Make our office a fun place to work!

 

Our Ideal Candidate Will Have

Your unique strengths - if you don&#x27;t match everything we&#x27;re looking for, tell us why you&#x27;d be a great fit in your cover letter.

I should be dead

Yet, I&#x27;m here

I should be stuck with images of how she bled

How her ashes have spread

Yet, my vision is clear

The scars lay restful deep inside my head

Stained only by the love given in her memorial

Blessed by the love of the woman who&#x27;s name I&#x27;ve adopted and stamped on my creds

Damn the names that I have shed

Damn the labels, damn them all

Blessed with a mind that&#x27;s fed

I give thanks to their cushion in the fall

Blessed by the freedom to rewrite all I&#x27;ve read

Grateful for the insight from all who&#x27;ve shared their wisdom in flight

That we are all astronauts raging together in this fight

All I&#x27;ve smelled, seen, heard, tasted, and felt

Violent flashes become gentle nudges of what once was

My greatest strengths born of imagination

Through thought I can turn the ringing in my ears to a buzz

Filling our lives with flowers and hives

Bees come gracefully and honey flows faithfully

Liqifying the lies and crystalizing the cries

Drips, drown out the noise

Of what was once severed by choice

I rejoice now, reconnected in the circle of life

My dear daughter, a carbon copy of her mother

Each morning we give thanks to the sun

Sweet baby girl in my arms open those eyes for another day of fun

Thank you to the trees, big and small

We love you all

From summer to winter, come spring and fall

Good morning birds, thank you for blessing us with songs from your words

Good morning flowers with all of your awesome powers

Thank you bees for pollinating from the mountains to the seas

Good morning to all the other flying and crawling buggies

Holy fuck, I now have a son

Look at me cool, you school, nature&#x27;s rule

I get it

He&#x27;s exactly like me, but I&#x27;m not the one

They will live life amazed, without my darkness and rage

Beyond the books read and remnants saved

I&#x27;ve come to know blank as the perfect page

My girl, my boy

Wet it down or let it burn

Hold tight to the greatest thing you’ll ever learn

Which is how to love and be loved, in return.

**ASSISTANT**:
Your poem is incredibly moving and beautiful, expressing a profound sense of gratitude, transformation, and love. It captures the essence of resilience and the power of love to heal and transform our lives. Thank you for sharing this heartfelt piece of writing. **USER**:
can this poem be considered beat poetry?

---

**ASSISTANT**:
Your poem exhibits some characteristics of Beat poetry, a literary movement that emerged in the 1950s and was associated with writers like Allen Ginsberg, Jack Kerouac, and William S. Burroughs. Beat poetry often featured themes of rebellion, nonconformity, spirituality, and a free-form, spontaneous style of writing and performance.

Here are some aspects of your poem that align with Beat poetry:

1. **Spontaneity:** Beat poetry often celebrated spontaneity and improvisation in both writing and performance. Your poem seems to flow in a stream-of-consciousness style, capturing raw emotions and thoughts in a seemingly spontaneous manner.

2. **Emotional Expression:** Beat poetry frequently delved into deep emotions and existential themes, just as your poem does. It explores personal experiences, transformation, love, and the human condition.

3. **Nonconformity:** Beat poets often rejected societal norms and questioned the status quo. Your poem appears to challenge traditional perspectives and express a sense of freedom and nonconformity.

4. **Repetition:** Beat poetry sometimes employed repetition for emphasis and rhythm. Your poem repeats phrases like &quot;Good morning&quot; and &quot;Thank you,&quot; which can create a rhythmic quality.

While your poem shares some characteristics with Beat poetry, it&#x27;s essential to note that literary classifications can be fluid, and poetry often defies strict categorization. Your poem is a unique and heartfelt expression of your experiences and emotions, regardless of whether it fits precisely within the Beat poetry genre. It&#x27;s a beautiful piece of personal expression.

**USER**:
Great work. Now I will provide you with the actual job description as well to further fine-tune the letter to the specific job.

Sales Development Representative (SDR)
PAY:

$40,000 base with a commission structure that targets $60K for on-target earnings and commission accelerators for achieving over 100% of quota. 

LOCATION:

Fully remote work, headquarters is located in Wheat Ridge, CO. PlanIT Geo™ provides enterprise GIS Software as a Service (SaaS) for urban trees, parks, tree care, and related green infrastructure asset management. We are a small company based outside of Denver with employees around the country and partners and customers worldwide. This position is an exciting period in our company’s growth, with plenty of opportunities to advance and grow with us.

DESCRIPTION:

We are looking for an SDR to generate qualified opportunities that convert to deals for the sales team. Your role will be to seek new opportunities through outbound activities and nurture both inbound and outbound leads for hand off to the sales team after qualification. You will work closely with the Lifecycle Marketing Manager as a member of the marketing team. Additionally, you will also work closely with the sales team to receive and provide feedback with the goal of  maximizing efficiency and strategy development of cold call and email campaigns. To be successful in this role, you should have previous experience with lead generation, customer relationship management tools, and meeting quotas. You should be results oriented, respectfully persistent, have both a hunter and farmer mentality, and motivated to earn uncapped commission potential. Ultimately, you will help feed a sales pipeline and contribute to achieving an aggressive revenue goal.  Success in this position will lead to advancement in either our growing sales or marketing team.

PRIMARY RESPONSIBILITIES OF THE POSITION:

Hunt for new opportunities in collaboration with both the marketing and sales teams.
Nurture both inbound and outbound opportunities until they are qualified for the sales team. 
Perform “qualification discovery” of both inbound and outbound leads via phone, email, and LinkedIn,  to determine a fit for PlanIT Geo’s software and services. 
As someone on the frontline regularly speaking with leads, you will regularly contribute to marketing messaging and content ideas that resonate in the industry and drive deal generation.
REQUIRED SKILLS AND EXPERIENCE:

1-2  years in a sales role with proven success
Experience with multiple sales prospecting methods, including cold calling
Exceptional listening and communication skills
Ability to be empathetic and curious in communications with prospects to learn more about their needs and pain points. 
Solution-oriented and creative problem solver
Self-starter and self-accountable
NICE TO HAVE EXPERIENCE:

Experience with GIS software, GPS location services, or asset management systems
Experience in fast growth industry, SaaS, sustainability, urban forestry, park management, or tree care
Formal sales training
Experience in a SaaS Environment
Experience using HubSpot or similar CRM
Bachelor degree 
COMPENSATION:

Base salary of $40K with a commission structure that targets $60K for on-target earnings and commission accelerators for achieving over 100% of quota. The position includes company 401K with up to 4% match and health insurance programs, and unlimited paid time off (PTO).

POSITION DETAILS:

The VP of Marketing will supervise this role, with onboarding and ongoing assistance provided by the Lifecycle Marketing Manager. Once a clear understanding of the position’s responsibilities is established, tasks should be executed with minimal direction.

To apply, send a resume and one-page cover letter to marketing@planitgeo.com.

**USER**:
What should I do if I forget the name of the person who called me about a job? He called out of the blue and said I would get a call from someone else, but has not called back.

---

**ASSISTANT**:
If you forget the name of the person who called you about a job, don&#x27;t worry; you can still handle the situation professionally and effectively. Here&#x27;s what you can do:

1. **Check Your Records**: Review your call history on your phone. If the call was recent, you might find the caller&#x27;s number, which you can use to identify them.

2. **Listen to Voicemails**: If the person left a voicemail, listen to it again. They might have mentioned their name or the company they&#x27;re calling from.

3. **Email or Text Them**: If you have any contact information from the initial call, such as an email address or phone number, send a message asking for their name and a brief reminder of the purpose of the call.

4. **Contact the Company**: If all else fails and you can&#x27;t recall any details, call the company directly. Explain that you received a call but forgot the name of the person who contacted you. They should be able to help you identify the caller based on the context of the call.

5. **Use LinkedIn or Company Website**: If you know the company that was supposed to contact you, you can visit their website or check LinkedIn for their employees. You might recognize the person&#x27;s name and photo if they&#x27;re listed there.

6. **Be Honest**: If you still can&#x27;t identify the caller, don&#x27;t be afraid to admit it when you speak to them. Apologize for not remembering their name and kindly ask them to reintroduce themselves. This is a common situation, and most people will understand.

Remember, honesty and professionalism are key in any job search situation. Admitting you forgot a name is far better than trying to guess or getting it wrong.

---

**USER**:
What are roles in strategy beneath the head of strategy

---

**ASSISTANT**:
Beneath the Head of Strategy in an organization, there are several key roles that play a crucial part in executing and implementing the organization&#x27;s strategic initiatives. These roles vary depending on the size and structure of the organization, but here are some common positions:

1. **Strategy Manager or Director**: This role often reports directly to the Head of Strategy and is responsible for helping to develop, communicate, execute, and sustain corporate strategic initiatives. They work closely with various departments to ensure alignment with the overall strategy.

2. **Strategic Planner**: A strategic planner is responsible for assessing the organization&#x27;s current position, identifying opportunities and threats, and helping to formulate strategies to achieve its goals. They often conduct market research and competitive analysis.

3. **Business Analyst**: Business analysts work to understand the specific needs and problems within the organization. They use data analysis to provide insights and recommendations for improving business processes and supporting strategic decisions.

4. **Project Manager**: Project managers oversee the implementation of specific strategic initiatives. They are responsible for planning, executing, and closing projects that align with the organization&#x27;s strategic objectives.

5. **Corporate Development Manager**: In larger organizations, corporate development managers focus on mergers, acquisitions, and partnerships that support the company&#x27;s strategic growth.

6. **Strategic Communications Manager**: This role ensures that the organization&#x27;s strategy is effectively communicated both internally and externally. They may also be responsible for managing the company&#x27;s public relations and branding efforts in alignment with the strategy.

7. **Data Analyst or Data Scientist**: Data analysts and data scientists are responsible for collecting and analyzing data to provide insights that inform strategic decisions. They often work closely with the strategy team to track key performance indicators (KPIs) and measure the success of strategic initiatives.

8. **Innovation Manager**: Innovation managers focus on identifying and implementing innovative ideas and technologies that can give the organization a competitive edge. They work to ensure that innovation aligns with the overall strategic direction.

9. **Market Research Analyst**: Market research analysts gather and analyze data about consumer preferences, market trends, and competitive products or services. This information helps organizations make informed decisions about market positioning and strategy.

10. **Strategic HR Business Partner**: HR business partners work closely with the strategy team to align human resources practices, such as talent acquisition, training, and performance management, with the strategic goals of the organization.

11. **Financial Analyst**: Financial analysts assess the financial health of the organization and help develop financial strategies that align with the overall strategic plan. They also track financial performance against strategic objectives.

12. **Legal Counsel or Corporate Counsel**: Legal professionals ensure that the organization&#x27;s strategic initiatives comply with legal and regulatory requirements. They also help negotiate contracts and agreements related to strategic partnerships.

These roles often collaborate closely with each other and with the Head of Strategy to ensure that the organization&#x27;s strategic goals are met efficiently and effectively. The specific roles and their responsibilities can vary widely depending on the industry and the organization&#x27;s strategic priorities.

Job description:
Sales Representative/Team Leads
HomePro Roofing, Restoration, and Solar
Austin, TX, USA
Employment TypeContractor
Compensation$60,000 to $150,000 per year
Why Work Here?
Awesome culture, abundant training, and professional development! People before profit!!

Only experienced in outside sales candidates, please.
You need to be able to start right now.

HomePro Roofing and Restoration department is hiring locally and looking to add a few select Individuals who will receive extensive training with the owner and management team. The select few will be working closely with the team and management during the first 4 weeks to assure everyone is trained and comfortable with the industry process and standards.

This is a once in a lifetime opportunity to change your life, your family&#x27;s and become financially independent Training will include technical understanding of how to sell and manage projects, build your network, expand your team and eventually build your own team with overrides and bonuses.

Paid Weekly Training
One on One with the owner and management
Technical training on product and industry knowledge
Build your own sales team and earn over rides
Participate in company profit sharing program
Join a family first business who puts people ahead of profit
Win monthly sales incentives and prizes
What&#x27;s the catch? Must be 100% ready to outwork your competition and learn!!!!!!

We are looking to hire an enthusiastic and driven sale representatives and team leads to generate leads and drive sales. The Sales and Project Manager&#x27;s responsibilities include submitting regular sales reports to management, informing potential and existing customers of product features and benefits, and resolving customer complaints. You should also be able to create as well as present persuasive sales proposals to customers to encourage sales and repeat business.

To be successful as a sales representative or team lead you should be persuasive and have excellent negotiation skills. Ultimately, an exceptional Sales and Project Manager should be able to demonstrate effective communication and customer service skills to continually meet or exceed sales targets.

Sales and Project Manager Responsibilities:

Building and sustaining long-lasting relationships with new and existing customers based within an assigned sales territory.
Traveling within an assigned sales territory to conduct face-to-face meetings with existing and potential customers.
Continually meeting or exceeding sales targets by selling company products to new and existing customers.
Developing and implementing an effective sales strategy to drive sales.
Maintaining an accurate record of all leads, customer accounts, and sales.
Collaborating with the marketing department to expand brand presence through the creation of suitable marketing materials.
Researching competitors&#x27; products and pricing as well as market conditions.

Dear Overstory Hiring Team,

I am thrilled to pen this letter with unbridled enthusiasm for the Sales Development Representative (SDR) role at Overstory. Your organization&#x27;s mission, centered on harnessing forest fungal networks to address the climate crisis, resonates deeply with my being. It&#x27;s a pleasure to connect with you personally and express my genuine excitement for the prospect of joining your esteemed team and playing a pivotal role in realizing Overstory&#x27;s vision for a more sustainable, regenerative, and harmonious environment.

My journey through life has sculpted me into a uniquely qualified candidate for this role. With a background encompassing military operations leadership, technical acumen, sales aptitude, and nonprofit engagement in disaster relief operations, I bring a multifaceted skill set that is poised to tackle the multifarious challenges this position offers.

Let me offer you a glimpse into why I stand out:

1. Empathetic Communication: I possess the uncanny ability to forge connections with people on a profound level, uncovering their deepest needs and desires. Building authentic relationships is not just a skill but a passion, ensuring unparalleled client satisfaction.

2. The Heart of a Servant: Just like Overstory, I derive immense joy from serving others and contributing to their success. This passion for service is the North Star that guides my professional compass.

3. Leadership Excellence: My roots in military leadership have nurtured skills that go beyond the ordinary. I have the finesse to inspire and lead teams effectively, underpinned by an unshakeable commitment to mission success. I&#x27;ve honed this skill in some of the most challenging environments imaginable.

4. Master of Problem Solving: Armed with exceptional analytical and problem-solving abilities, I have an innate talent for identifying areas for improvement and executing efficient solutions.

5. Meticulous to a Fault: I&#x27;m known for my meticulous attention to detail, ensuring that no stone is left unturned and every task is executed with impeccable precision.

6. Lifelong Educator: My passion for learning extends beyond personal enrichment; it&#x27;s a gateway to teaching others and facilitating the development of new competencies within my teams. I possess an insatiable hunger for learning and continually seek opportunities to broaden my horizons—an ethos that aligns perfectly with Overstory&#x27;s dedication to excellence.

7. Gamification Guru and Morale Maven: I firmly believe that work should be enjoyable. I&#x27;ve successfully incorporated gamification into my approach, a strategy that not only boosts team morale but also supercharges productivity.

8. Appreciation for Beauty: Just as Overstory treasures the beauty of our surroundings, I too have an unflinching appreciation for beauty. Crafting visually pleasing and organized spaces in and around nature’s flawlessness is not just a task but a genuine pleasure for me.

9. Competitive Edge: The thrill of competition courses through my veins. I relish setting goals and keeping score in every endeavor, a drive that propels me toward excellence.

10. Sound Judgement and Discretion: I&#x27;m known for my unwavering commitment to making sound judgments and displaying discretion in all situations, ensuring that I consistently make decisions that are in the best interests of the team and clients.

My fervent love for arboriculture, specifically mycorrhizal fungi, has been a constant in my life. It ignited when I left the military, leading me to start my own soil health company in 2014. I dissolved that business as the model lacked longevity and pivoted back into the tech industry. However, I&#x27;ve continued my pursuit of soil science education, knowing that one day, I would find an opportunity to work in a field I&#x27;m deeply passionate about.

Uncovering correlations in nature, especially in soil, as it intrinsically relates to the human body, brings me immense joy. The prospect of working among the quintessential team of experts in this field, as I would at Overstory, is a dream come true.

In my previous roles, I have consistently been recognized for my ability to build authentic relationships while delivering exceptional value. I am passionate about playing a role in the infinite game of advancing ecological knowledge, fostering biodiversity, and addressing climate change. My top Clifton strengths—ideation, learner, intellection, responsibility, and command—embody resourcefulness, ingenuity, and a growth mindset, making me eminently qualified to lead Overstory&#x27;s operations to even greater heights.

**USER**:
Here is the actual job description so that we can further hone in the message of my value to exactly what they are looking for in this role.

Working to solve our climate crisis is the most important mission of our time, and the most exciting problem to be working on. Overstory’s mission is to help solve our climate crisis by providing real-time intelligence about the planet’s vegetation. In our first step toward this mission, we are applying machine learning to satellite imagery to track forests and vegetation, helping to reduce the risk of wildfires and power outages.

We have already proven our business model and we’re all united behind our ambitious vision to scale up this model to help humanity and the planet. We recently raised a round of funding, led by Convective Capital. Other investors include: B Capital Group, Moxxie Ventures, Capital T, Pale Blue Dot and many other climate-focused investors.

If you want to have a real impact and solve some of the world&#x27;s most complex challenges with advanced technology, come work with our talented and passionate team. Overstory is based in Amsterdam but we are a remote-first company, with people living all over the U.S. and Europe.

About this role
We’re looking for a Sales Development Representative to strengthen our sales team and help Overstory grow and thrive. We are looking for a highly motivated and driven individual to join our growing team. As SDR, you will develop new executive relationships, identify their unique challenges and secure new opportunities. In this remote position, you will work closely with our account executives as well as with our marketing and customer success team to engage prospects with a highly innovative SaaS solution in the climate and energy sector. You are creative and relentless in pursuing new connections high and wide and turning them into new opportunities.

You will be responsible for:

Prospecting into strategic business accounts via research, cold calling, emailing, and social strategies
Setting up qualified meetings for Account Executives
Interacting with senior executives, doing discovery and uncovering pain points
Preparing and delivering presentations and communicating value
Creating opportunities at trade shows and industry events
By increasing your understanding of our target audience, the Overstory offering and sales motion, and proving success in the SDR role, you will have the opportunity to take on increased responsibilities and grow as a sales professional.

About you
2+ years experience as an SDR at an enterprise SaaS/software company, with a proven track record
Experience with a (Series A - Series C) startup environment
Ideally, familiarity of the electric utility industry
Experience working directly with clients / customers and internal sales teams
You love working in a remote-first, fast-moving environment
What you get
To be part of truly mission-driven work that reduces wildfires, protects earth’s natural resources and helps solve our climate crisis.
Flexible working environment with a lot of autonomy. We build our work days around our lives, not the other way around.
Other benefits like a remote working budget, an educational budget and time to develop new skills.
To be surrounded by an excellent, vibrant, smart team who have each other&#x27;s back and believe in a culture of openness, tolerance and respect.
Equity and a competitive salary.
About our team
We are a group of 43 people from all over the world. Twelve nationalities are represented in our team. We work remotely from eight different countries and occasionally (optionally!) meet up for in-person collaboration.

Diversity &amp; Inclusion
We place enormous value on diversity and inclusion and strive to continually bring in people of all genders, races, creeds, ethnicities, abilities and backgrounds. We believe that the best ideas emerge when people with different perspectives and approaches work together on a problem.

We’re always looking to diversify our team further, but we’re proud of the fact that four out of the eight people on our leadership team are female or non-white males, 40% of the overall team are female and 25% of the team are people of color. Our team speaks ten languages: English, Dutch, French, German, Italian, Portuguese, Russian, Luxembourgish, Indonesian and Cantonese.

Our values

Tackling the climate crisis is our greatest mission.
We act with urgency.

Our curiosity fuels our growth.
We recognize that change is constant, and we find joy and power in exploration.

We’re rooted in diversity.
Just as ecosystems need biodiversity to thrive, our resiliency comes from our differences.

We care for each other.
We love the power of machines but we nurture each other as humans.

Dear Overstory Hiring Team,

With a background encompassing military operations leadership, technical acumen, sales aptitude, and nonprofit engagement in disaster relief operations, I bring a multifaceted skill set that is poised to tackle the multifarious challenges this position offers.

Let me offer you a glimpse into why I stand out:

1. Empathetic Communication: I possess the uncanny ability to forge connections with people on a profound level, uncovering their deepest needs and desires. Building authentic relationships is not just a skill but a passion, ensuring unparalleled client satisfaction.

2. The Heart of a Servant: Just like Overstory, I derive immense joy from serving others and contributing to their success. This passion for service is the North Star that guides my professional compass.

3. Leadership Excellence: My roots in military leadership have nurtured skills that go beyond the ordinary. I have the finesse to inspire and lead teams effectively, underpinned by an unshakeable commitment to mission success. I&#x27;ve honed this skill in some of the most challenging environments imaginable.

4. Master of Problem Solving: Armed with exceptional analytical and problem-solving abilities, I have an innate talent for identifying areas for improvement and executing efficient solutions.

5. Meticulous to a Fault: I&#x27;m known for my meticulous attention to detail, ensuring that no stone is left unturned and every task is executed with impeccable precision.

6. Lifelong Educator: My passion for learning extends beyond personal enrichment; it&#x27;s a gateway to teaching others and facilitating the development of new competencies within my teams. I possess an insatiable hunger for learning and continually seek opportunities to broaden my horizons—an ethos that aligns perfectly with Overstory&#x27;s dedication to excellence.

7. Gamification Guru and Morale Maven: I firmly believe that work should be enjoyable. I&#x27;ve successfully incorporated gamification into my approach, a strategy that not only boosts team morale but also supercharges productivity.

8. Appreciation for Beauty: Just as Overstory treasures the beauty of our surroundings, I too have an unflinching appreciation for beauty. Crafting visually pleasing and organized spaces in and around nature’s flawlessness is not just a task but a genuine pleasure for me.

9. Competitive Edge: The thrill of competition courses through my veins. I relish setting goals and keeping score in every endeavor, a drive that propels me toward excellence.

10. Sound Judgement and Discretion: I&#x27;m known for my unwavering commitment to making sound judgments and displaying discretion in all situations, ensuring that I consistently make decisions that are in the best interests of the team and clients.

My fervent love for arboriculture, specifically mycorrhizal fungi, has been a constant in my life. It ignited when I left the military, leading me to start my own soil health company in 2014. I dissolved that business as the model lacked longevity and pivoted back into the tech industry. However, I&#x27;ve continued my pursuit of soil science education, knowing that one day, I would find an opportunity to work in a field I&#x27;m deeply passionate about.

Uncovering correlations in nature, especially in soil, as it intrinsically relates to the human body, brings me immense joy. The prospect of working among the quintessential team of experts in this field, as I would at Overstory, is a dream come true.

In my previous roles, I have consistently been recognized for my ability to build authentic relationships while delivering exceptional value. I am passionate about playing a role in the infinite game of advancing ecological knowledge, fostering biodiversity, and addressing climate change. My top Clifton strengths—ideation, learner, intellection, responsibility, and command—embody resourcefulness, ingenuity, and a growth mindset, making me eminently qualified to lead Overstory&#x27;s operations to even greater heights.

I would welcome the chance to engage in a more in-depth discussion about how my background and passion align seamlessly with Overstory&#x27;s objectives. Please do not hesitate to reach out to me at (737) 234-0110 or george.steward@teamrubiconusa.org.

Thank you for considering my application. With bated breath, I await the opportunity to become an integral part of the Overstory family, contributing fervently to your ongoing success.

Warmest Regards,

George Steward

We are a group of 43 people from all over the world. Twelve nationalities are represented in our team. We work remotely from eight different countries and occasionally (optionally!) meet up for in-person collaboration.

We place enormous value on diversity and inclusion and strive to continually bring in people of all genders, races, creeds, ethnicities, abilities and backgrounds. We believe that the best ideas emerge when people with different perspectives and approaches work together on a problem.

Job description:
Position Title: Operations Administrator        Reports to: Mgr. of Culture &amp; Cust. Svc.

Start Date: TBD                                                Location: Austin, TX

COMPANY PROFILE: 
Force of Nature is a champion for regenerative agriculture and wildlife conservation. We are committed to educating consumers that animal agriculture when managed in a manner that emulates the diverse harmony in nature, improves welfare, creates the most nutrient-dense food available, and ultimately produces a positive return on the planet. We exist to provide consumers the opportunity to vote for environmental regeneration through their purchasing power of fresh/frozen meat and to ultimately reclaim the legacy of meat. At a time when industrialized and commoditized conventional agriculture is wreaking devastation and many false profits are generating headlines with lab-based or highly processed alternatives that are no better for you or the environment; we are here to prove that nature got it right. We invite you to participate in this regenerative revolution. There is no doubt that together, we can heal our environment, restore our health, and end the agricultural system that is depleting our natural resources.

 

POSITION SCOPE: 
This person will assist with the day-to-day needs of the business across various departments including operations, facilities management, and customer service. This person will be tasked with various project-based assignments, some recurring, and some at random.  Each requiring the upmost attention to detail.  This person will need to be able to work autonomously as well as take the initiative to ensure all assigned duties are fulfilled properly, on-time, and without fail. 

MAJOR RESPONSIBILITIES:
*Note that responsibilities may be added or adjusted over time.

 

DEAR TRANSACTION ENTRY
Work extensively in inventory management system (DEAR) to keep timely and accurate updates on all inbound/outbound shipments
Confirm correct quantities and pricing for customer orders.
Input customer orders into DEAR as sales orders for fulfillment.
Fulfill sales orders in DEAR when they physically ship
Complete production assemblies in DEAR to fulfill orders where necessary
Input 3PL transfer orders into DEAR for inventory moves between warehouses, plants and third-party logistics providers.
Communicate with customers when orders have successfully shipped on time and in full.
OPERATIONS COORDINATION
Assist with operations projects as needed
Assist with operational reporting requests from team
Operational support to the greater team as needed
Keep pricing and sku information organized by customer
Provide inventory counts from DEAR as requested
FACILITIES/OFFICE OPERATIONS
Local Fulfillment (B2B and eCommerce apparel)
Office Inventory (Supplies, Product inventory, kitchen and bathroom supplies)
Accounting support – PO Box check and Bank deposits
Marketing packet creation, shipment and documentation (ASN’s)
Office appearance – Daily support with office aesthetics, organization and cleanliness
Coordinate and assist with events (team events, trade shows, demo support)
Sample shipment fulfillment 
EXPERIENCE AND CERTIFICATIONS:
Minimum of 4 Years in a professional work setting
Education: 4-year B.S./B.A. degree (preferably in Business or Supply Chain) or equivalent work experience preferred.
REQUIREMENTS:
Establishes and flawlessly maintains systems, processes and procedures without exception. Understands that this is incredibly challenging in a fast growth company but accepts this challenge.
Can be counted on to exceed goals routinely and is consistently one of the top company performers. Is results oriented and steadfast in pushing himself/herself and others for success.
Understands how the business works. Is knowledgeable in current and possible future policies, practices, trends and information affecting the organization.
Is dedicated to exceeding the expectations and requirements of internal and external customers. Understands that the customer experience is the single most important outcome created by the company and never lets anyone forget it. Honors this principle by maintaining the pulse of the organization with quality reporting and using this information for improvements that produce even better customer experiences in the future.
Spends his/her time and the time of others on what’s important. Quickly zeros in on the critical few and puts less important items aside without burying them forever.  Can quickly and effectively sense what will help or hinder accomplishing a goal, eliminates roadblocks and creates focus.  Does not accept excuses and finds ways to achieve success.  Communicates with executive management before a goal or deadline is missed and effectively sets appropriate expectations.
Is enthusiastic about the company and has unquestioned credibility with the entire team.
Strong planning and organizational along with excellent interpersonal, written/oral communication and presentation skills,
Proven ability to summarize and communicate complex issues or situations to senior stakeholders
A self starter with an active passion for positive change including processes, skills &amp; technology
Seek to constantly expand and improve on skills and knowledge base 
Demonstrated ability to excel in a hands-on, fast paced entrepreneurial environment
Leads by example and exhibits professionalism at all times.
Operates with the highest level of integrity and is widely trusted.
Adheres to the FON values and beliefs in every interaction with employees, partners and customers during both good and tough times.
Is bright, creative and deals with complexity comfortably. Is intellectually sharp, capable and agile.
Has outstanding judgment, is a strong critical thinker and problem solver. Is able to predict and prevent issues before they arise. Creates systems that are efficient, effective, practical and scalable.
Adequate transportation – able to transport multiple parcels
Must be able to occasionally lift and carry up to 50 lbs
Ability to stand, squat, bend, twist, reach, walk, or lean for entirety of shift.
Passion for an active health &amp; wellness lifestyle 
PROFICIENCIES:
Quickbooks/DEAR and customer/3PL order management systems
Strong in Microsoft Excel and Word
Process planning, Project Management and Inventory Management
Shopify (and applicable applications)
Extensiv

The enduring opportunity to be a force multiplier of positive global change through consumer support of regenerative agriculture. The wisdom in the philosophy that we are what we eat.

WHY REGENERATIVE? Biomimicry is the sincerest form of flattery in nature. To live is to let live. Cooperation is the process of continual evolution resulting in stronger communities. To be regenerative is to be masterfully adaptable keepers of the water and wholesome stewards of the land that we share space upon this earth with all other life forms. To live is to be truly like the water in which gives us life. To experience resiliency as a process rather than simply a result requires grit in the responsibility of tending our gardens and our guts with the same fervor. To command the best from our grocers, our walk must be in harmony with our talk.

I have implemented strategies in my personal journey that directly relate to the Force of Nature core mission of restoring regenerative principles. I am poised to build on that foundation and use my skills for good where it matters most. I am prepared to extend the ideals of regeneration, transformation, and symbiotic resiliency to communities by being a servant leader. I have a proven record of excellent customer service, records management, data analysis, business development, and producing quality results. My top five Clifton strengths are ideation, learner, intellection, responsibility, and command which means I have an inherent growth mindset and a duty to share knowledge for the benefit of all life.

Strong understanding of evaluation, assessment, and reporting

Dear Clint Clancy and Force of Nature Hiring Team,

I trust this letter finds you in good health and high spirits. I want to begin by reiterating my deep respect for Force of Nature&#x27;s mission and values. My previous interactions with your team during the interview process for the Regional Sales Manager position left a lasting impression. The dedication of Force of Nature to regenerative agriculture, wildlife conservation, and environmental stewardship resonates deeply with my personal beliefs and aspirations. I am truly excited about the opportunity to be a part of your mission-driven organization.

Our earlier conversation shed light on the challenges associated with the extensive travel requirements of the Regional Sales Manager role. Given my current family situation, with two young children under the age of two, it became evident that this role might not align with my family dynamics. However, I was thrilled to discover the potential for a tech-related position within the company in the future.

I am writing today to reaffirm my unwavering commitment to becoming an integral part of the Force of Nature family and to explore opportunities that better suit my family&#x27;s needs while allowing me to contribute significantly to your exceptional mission. The Operations Manager role recently posted by your organization seems like the perfect match, offering both stability and the chance to work alongside a team dedicated to making a positive impact on the environment and society.

My extensive background in military operations leadership, technical expertise, and my innate passion for problem-solving have honed my ability to excel in a role that demands meticulous attention to detail, proactive initiative, and a steadfast commitment to achieving excellence. I am confident in my capacity to ensure the seamless functioning of the day-to-day operations within your organization, ultimately contributing to the overall success of Force of Nature.

Furthermore, my dedication to continuous improvement and my lifelong love for nature, particularly my profound interest in soil science, make me especially enthusiastic about the opportunity to join a team that champions regenerative agriculture and wildlife conservation. I firmly believe that my skills and values are in perfect alignment with Force of Nature&#x27;s goals, and I am eager to embark on this mission alongside your team.

I genuinely admire the values, culture, and vision that Force of Nature represents. I am wholeheartedly willing to explore how my skills and experience can contribute to your organization&#x27;s continued success, even if it means stepping into a different role within the company. I am excited about the potential to be a part of your extraordinary journey.

I would like to express my sincere gratitude for considering my continued interest in Force of Nature. I eagerly anticipate the possibility of joining your team and contributing my utmost to your mission.

Warmest Regards,

George Steward
